    <article class="markdown-body entry-content p-3 p-md-6" itemprop="text"><p align="center">
  <a href="https://github.com/trimstray/the-book-of-secret-knowledge">
    <img src="https://github.com/trimstray/the-book-of-secret-knowledge/raw/master/static/img/the-book-of-secret-knowledge-preview.png" alt="Master" style="max-width:100%;">
  </a>
</p>
<p align="center">"<i>Knowledge is powerful, be careful how you use it!</i>"</p>
<h4 align="center"><a id="user-content-a-collection-of-inspiring-lists-manuals-cheatsheets-blogs-hacks-one-liners-cliweb-tools-and-more" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#a-collection-of-inspiring-lists-manuals-cheatsheets-blogs-hacks-one-liners-cliweb-tools-and-more"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>A collection of inspiring lists, manuals, cheatsheets, blogs, hacks, one-liners, cli/web tools, and more.</h4>
<br>
<p align="center">
  <a href="https://github.com/trimstray/the-book-of-secret-knowledge/pulls">
    <img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/97d6177a812e2302a8b9953c731d57c58aa4ca88/68747470733a2f2f696d672e736869656c64732e696f2f62616467652f5052732d77656c636f6d652d627269676874677265656e2e7376673f6c6f6e6743616368653d74727565" alt="Pull Requests" data-canonical-src="https://img.shields.io/badge/PRs-welcome-brightgreen.svg?longCache=true" style="max-width:100%;">

<h2><a id="user-content-notebook_with_decorative_cover-what-is-it" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#notebook_with_decorative_cover-what-is-it"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="notebook_with_decorative_cover" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f4d4.png">ð</g-emoji> Â What is it?</h2>
<p>This repository is a collection of various materials and tools that I use every day in my work. It contains a lot of useful information gathered in one piece. It is an invaluable source of knowledge for me that I often look back on.</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-restroom-for-whom" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#restroom-for-whom"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="restroom" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f6bb.png">ð»</g-emoji> Â For whom?</h2>
<p>For everyone, really. Here everyone can find their favourite tastes. But to be perfectly honest, it is aimed towards System and Network administrators, DevOps, Pentesters, and Security Researchers.</p>
<h2><a id="user-content-information_source-contributing" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#information_source-contributing"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a><g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="information_source" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/2139.png">â¹ï¸</g-emoji> Â Contributing</h2>
<p>If you find something which doesn't make sense, or something doesn't seem right, please make a pull request and please add valid and well-reasoned explanations about your changes or comments.</p>
<p>A few simple rules for this project:</p>
<ul>
<li>inviting and clear</li>
<li>not tiring</li>
<li>useful</li>
</ul>
<p>These below rules may be better:</p>
<ul>
<li>easy to contribute to (Markdown + HTML ...)</li>
<li>easy to find (simple TOC, maybe it's worth extending them?)</li>
</ul>
<p>Url marked <strong>*</strong> is temporary unavailable. Please don't delete it without confirming that it has permanently expired.</p>
<p>Before adding a pull request, please see the <strong><a href="/trimstray/the-book-of-secret-knowledge/blob/master/.github/CONTRIBUTING.md">contributing guidelines</a></strong>. You should also remember about this:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-diff"><pre><span class="pl-mi1"><span class="pl-mi1">+</span> This repository is not meant to contain everything but only good quality stuff.</span></pre></div>
<p>All <strong>suggestions/PR</strong> are welcome!</p>
<h3><a id="user-content-code-contributors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#code-contributors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Code Contributors</h3>
<p>This project exists thanks to all the people who contribute.</p>
<p><a href="https://github.com/trimstray/the-book-of-secret-knowledge/graphs/contributors"><img src="https://camo.githubusercontent.com/53797ef705982dc848e3a3f0b75298ad71a24e25/68747470733a2f2f6f70656e636f6c6c6563746976652e636f6d2f7468652d626f6f6b2d6f662d7365637265742d6b6e6f776c656467652f636f6e7472696275746f72732e7376673f77696474683d38393026627574746f6e3d66616c7365" data-canonical-src="https://opencollective.com/the-book-of-secret-knowledge/contributors.svg?width=890&amp;button=false" style="max-width:100%;"></a></p>
<h3><a id="user-content-financial-contributors" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#financial-contributors"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Financial Contributors</h3>

<p>
Â Â <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="small_orange_diamond" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f538.png">ð¸</g-emoji> <a href="https://www.gnu.org/software/bash/" rel="nofollow"><b>GNU Bash</b></a> - is an sh-compatible shell that incorporates useful features from the Korn shell and C shell.<br>
Â Â <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="small_orange_diamond" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f538.png">ð¸</g-emoji> <a href="https://www.zsh.org/" rel="nofollow"><b>Zsh</b></a> - is a shell designed for interactive use, although it is also a powerful scripting language.<br>
Â Â <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="small_orange_diamond" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f538.png">ð¸</g-emoji> <a href="https://tcl-lang.org/" rel="nofollow"><b>tclsh</b></a> - is a very powerful cross-platform shell, suitable for a huge range of uses.<br>
Â Â <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="small_orange_diamond" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f538.png">ð¸</g-emoji> <a href="https://github.com/Bash-it/bash-it"><b>bash-it</b></a> - is a framework for using, developing and maintaining shell scripts and custom commands.<br>
Â Â <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="small_orange_diamond" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f538.png">ð¸</g-emoji> <a href="https://ohmyz.sh/" rel="nofollow"><b>Oh My ZSH!</b></a> - is the best framework for managing your Zsh configuration.<br>
Â Â <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="small_orange_diamond" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f538.png">ð¸</g-emoji> <a href="https://github.com/oh-my-fish/oh-my-fish"><b>Oh My Fish</b></a> - the Fishshell framework.<br>

<p>
Â Â <g-emoji class="g-emoji" alias="small_orange_diamond" fallback-src="https://github.githubassets.com/images/icons/emoji/unicode/1f538.png">ð¸</g-emoji> <a href="https://github.com/rupa/z"><b>z</b></a> - tracks the folder you use the most and allow you to jump, without having to type the whole path.<br>

<h6><a id="user-content-hack-mozilla-firefox-addressbar" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#hack-mozilla-firefox-addressbar"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Hack Mozilla Firefox addressbar</h6>
<p>In Firefox's addressbar, you can limit results by typing special characters before or after your term:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>^</code> - for matches in your browsing history</li>
<li><code>*</code> - for matches in your bookmarks.</li>
<li><code>%</code> - for matches in your currently open tabs.</li>
<li><code>#</code> - for matches in page titles.</li>
<li><code>@</code> - for matches in web addresses.</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-bypass-wafs-by-shortening-ip-address-by-0xinfection" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#bypass-wafs-by-shortening-ip-address-by-0xinfection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Bypass WAFs by Shortening IP Address (by <a href="https://twitter.com/0xInfection" rel="nofollow">0xInfection</a>)</h6>
<p>IP addresses can be shortened by dropping the zeroes:</p>
<pre><code>http://1.0.0.1 â http://1.1
http://127.0.0.1 â http://127.1
http://192.168.0.1 â http://192.168.1

http://0xC0A80001 or http://3232235521 â 192.168.0.1
http://192.168.257 â 192.168.1.1
http://192.168.516 â 192.168.2.4
</code></pre>
<blockquote>
<p>This bypasses WAF filters for SSRF, open-redirect, etc where any IP as input gets blacklisted.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>For more information please see <a href="http://www.pc-help.org/obscure.htm" rel="nofollow">How to Obscure Any URL</a> and <a href="https://stuff-things.net/2014/09/25/magic-ip-address-shortcuts/" rel="nofollow">Magic IP Address Shortcuts</a>.</p>
<h4><a id="user-content-one-liners-toc" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#one-liners-toc"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>One-liners Â <a href="#anger-table-of-contents"><sup>[TOC]</sup></a></h4>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-terminal" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-terminal"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Linux_console" rel="nofollow">terminal</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-reload-shell-without-exit" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#reload-shell-without-exit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Reload shell without exit</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">exec</span> <span class="pl-smi">$SHELL</span> -l</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-close-shell-keeping-all-subprocess-running" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#close-shell-keeping-all-subprocess-running"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Close shell keeping all subprocess running</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">disown</span> -a <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-c1">exit</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-exit-without-saving-shell-history" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#exit-without-saving-shell-history"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Exit without saving shell history</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">kill</span> -9 <span class="pl-smi">$$</span>
<span class="pl-c1">unset</span> HISTFILE <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-c1">exit</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-perform-a-branching-conditional" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#perform-a-branching-conditional"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Perform a branching conditional</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-pipe-stdout-and-stderr-to-separate-commands" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#pipe-stdout-and-stderr-to-separate-commands"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Pipe stdout and stderr to separate commands</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>some_command <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&gt;(</span>/bin/cmd_for_stdout<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span> <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&gt;(</span>/bin/cmd_for_stderr<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-redirect-stdout-and-stderr-each-to-separate-files-and-print-both-to-the-screen" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#redirect-stdout-and-stderr-each-to-separate-files-and-print-both-to-the-screen"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Redirect stdout and stderr each to separate files and print both to the screen</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>(some_command <span class="pl-k">2&gt;&amp;1</span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;3</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> tee errorlog ) <span class="pl-k">3&gt;&amp;1</span> <span class="pl-k">1&gt;&amp;2</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> tee stdoutlog</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-list-of-commands-you-use-most-often" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#list-of-commands-you-use-most-often"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>List of commands you use most often</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">history</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{CMD[$2]++;count++;}END { for (a in CMD)print CMD[a] " " CMD[a]/count*100 "% " a;}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
grep -v <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>./<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
column -c3 -s <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -t <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sort -nr <span class="pl-k">|</span> nl <span class="pl-k">|</span>  head -n 20</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-sterilize-bash-history" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#sterilize-bash-history"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Sterilize bash history</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">sterile()</span> {

  <span class="pl-c1">history</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>$2 != "history" { $1=""; print $0 }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> egrep -vi <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">curl\b+.*(-E|--cert)\b+.*\b*|<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">curl\b+.*--pass\b+.*\b*|<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">curl\b+.*(-U|--proxy-user).*:.*\b*|<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">curl\b+.*(-u|--user).*:.*\b*</span>
<span class="pl-s">.*(-H|--header).*(token|auth.*)\b+.*|<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">wget\b+.*--.*password\b+.*\b*|<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">http.?://.+:.+@.*<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/histbuff<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">history</span> -r <span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/histbuff<span class="pl-k">;</span>

}

<span class="pl-k">export</span> PROMPT_COMMAND=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>sterile<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<blockquote>
<p>Look also: <a href="https://github.com/lbonanomi/go/blob/master/revisionist.go">A naive utility to censor credentials in command history</a>.</p>
</blockquote>

<h6><a id="user-content-create-a-directory-and-change-into-it-at-the-same-time" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#create-a-directory-and-change-into-it-at-the-same-time"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Create a directory and change into it at the same time</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-print-a-row-of-characters-across-the-terminal" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-a-row-of-characters-across-the-terminal"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print a row of characters across the terminal</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>%<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">`</span>tput cols<span class="pl-pds">`</span></span>s<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> tr <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>#<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-shell-history-without-line-numbers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-shell-history-without-line-numbers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show shell history without line numbers</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">history</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> cut -c 8-
<span class="pl-c1">fc</span> -l -n 1 <span class="pl-k">|</span> sed <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/^\s*//<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-run-commands-after-exit-session" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#run-commands-after-exit-session"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Run command(s) after exit session</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>cat <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> /etc/profile <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">_after_logout() {</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">  username=$(whoami)</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">  for _pid in $(ps afx | grep sshd | grep "$username" | awk '{print $1}') ; do</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    kill -9 $_pid</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">  done</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">}</span>
<span class="pl-s">trap _after_logout EXIT</span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-a-sequence-of-numbers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-a-sequence-of-numbers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate a sequence of numbers</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">((</span>i<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">1</span>; i<span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>; i<span class="pl-k">+=</span><span class="pl-c1">2</span><span class="pl-pds">))</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-smi">$i</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> alternative: seq 1 2 10</span>

<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">((</span>i<span class="pl-k">=</span><span class="pl-c1">5</span>; i<span class="pl-k">&lt;=</span><span class="pl-c1">10</span>; <span class="pl-k">++</span>i<span class="pl-pds">))</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> <span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%02d\n<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-smi">$i</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> alternative: seq -w 5 10</span>

<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> {1..10} <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-smi">$i</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-simple-bash-filewatching" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#simple-bash-filewatching"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Simple Bash filewatching</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">unset</span> MAIL<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">export</span> MAILCHECK=1<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">export</span> MAILPATH=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>$FILE_TO_WATCH?$MESSAGE<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-busybox" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-busybox"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.busybox.net/" rel="nofollow">busybox</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-static-http-web-server" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#static-http-web-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Static HTTP web server</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-mount-a-temporary-ram-partition" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#mount-a-temporary-ram-partition"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Mount a temporary ram partition</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-show-which-processes-use-the-filesdirectories" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-which-processes-use-the-filesdirectories"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show which processes use the files/directories</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-kills-a-process-that-is-locking-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#kills-a-process-that-is-locking-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Kills a process that is locking a file</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-kills-a-process-that-is-locking-a-file-with-specific-signal" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#kills-a-process-that-is-locking-a-file-with-specific-signal"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Kills a process that is locking a file with specific signal</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-show-process-that-use-internet-connection-at-the-moment" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-process-that-use-internet-connection-at-the-moment"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show process that use internet connection at the moment</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-lists-all-listening-ports-together-with-the-pid-of-the-associated-process" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#lists-all-listening-ports-together-with-the-pid-of-the-associated-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Lists all listening ports together with the PID of the associated process</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-list-all-open-ports-and-their-owning-executables" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#list-all-open-ports-and-their-owning-executables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>List all open ports and their owning executables</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>lsof -i -P <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -i <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>listen<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-all-open-ports" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-all-open-ports"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show all open ports</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>lsof -Pnl -i</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-open-ports-listen" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-open-ports-listen"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show open ports (LISTEN)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>lsof -Pni4 <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep LISTEN <span class="pl-k">|</span> column -t</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-list-all-files-opened-by-a-particular-command" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#list-all-files-opened-by-a-particular-command"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>List all files opened by a particular command</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>lsof -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>process<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-view-user-activity-per-directory" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#view-user-activity-per-directory"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>View user activity per directory</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>lsof -u username -a +D /etc</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-10-largest-open-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-10-largest-open-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show 10 largest open files</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>lsof / <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{ if($7 &gt; 1048576) print $7/1048576 "MB" " " $9 " " $1 }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sort -n -u <span class="pl-k">|</span> tail <span class="pl-k">|</span> column -t</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-current-working-directory-of-a-process" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-current-working-directory-of-a-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show current working directory of a process</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>lsof -p <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>PID<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep cwd</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-ps" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-ps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ps_(Unix)" rel="nofollow">ps</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-a-4-way-scrollable-process-tree-with-full-details" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-a-4-way-scrollable-process-tree-with-full-details"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show a 4-way scrollable process tree with full details</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ps awwfux <span class="pl-k">|</span> less -S</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-processes-per-user-counter" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#processes-per-user-counter"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Processes per user counter</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ps hax -o user <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort <span class="pl-k">|</span> uniq -c <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort -r</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-all-processes-by-name-with-main-header" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-all-processes-by-name-with-main-header"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show all processes by name with main header</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ps -lfC nginx</pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-find" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-find"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Find_(Unix)" rel="nofollow">find</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-find-files-that-have-been-modified-on-your-system-in-the-past-60-minutes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#find-files-that-have-been-modified-on-your-system-in-the-past-60-minutes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Find files that have been modified on your system in the past 60 minutes</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find / -mmin 60 -type f</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-find-all-files-larger-than-20m" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#find-all-files-larger-than-20m"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Find all files larger than 20M</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find / -type f -size +20M</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-find-duplicate-files-based-on-md5-hash" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#find-duplicate-files-based-on-md5-hash"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Find duplicate files (based on MD5 hash)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find -type f -exec md5sum <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>;<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort <span class="pl-k">|</span> uniq --all-repeated=separate -w 33</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-change-permission-only-for-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#change-permission-only-for-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Change permission only for files</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> /var/www/site <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -type f -exec chmod 766 {} <span class="pl-cce">\;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> /var/www/site <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -type f -exec chmod 664 {} +</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-change-permission-only-for-directories" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#change-permission-only-for-directories"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Change permission only for directories</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> /var/www/site <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -type d -exec chmod g+x {} <span class="pl-cce">\;</span>
<span class="pl-c1">cd</span> /var/www/site <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -type d -exec chmod g+rwx {} +</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-find-files-and-directories-for-specific-user" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#find-files-and-directories-for-specific-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Find files and directories for specific user</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -user <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>username<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> -print</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-find-files-and-directories-for-all-without-specific-user" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#find-files-and-directories-for-all-without-specific-user"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Find files and directories for all without specific user</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> <span class="pl-cce">\!</span>-user <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>username<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> -print</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-delete-older-files-than-60-days" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#delete-older-files-than-60-days"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Delete older files than 60 days</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -type f -mtime +60 -delete</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-recursively-remove-all-empty-sub-directories-from-a-directory" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recursively-remove-all-empty-sub-directories-from-a-directory"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Recursively remove all empty sub-directories from a directory</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -depth  -type d  -empty -exec rmdir {} <span class="pl-cce">\;</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-how-to-find-all-hard-links-to-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#how-to-find-all-hard-links-to-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>How to find all hard links to a file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>/path/to/dir<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> -xdev -samefile filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-recursively-find-the-latest-modified-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recursively-find-the-latest-modified-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Recursively find the latest modified files</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -type f -exec stat --format <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%Y :%y %n<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>{}<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-cce">\;</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort -nr <span class="pl-k">|</span> cut -d: -f2- <span class="pl-k">|</span> head</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-recursively-findreplace-of-a-string-with-sed" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recursively-findreplace-of-a-string-with-sed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Recursively find/replace of a string with sed</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -not -path <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>*/\.git*<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -type f -print0 <span class="pl-k">|</span> xargs -0 sed -i <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/foo/bar/g<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-recursively-findreplace-of-a-string-in-directories-and-file-names" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recursively-findreplace-of-a-string-in-directories-and-file-names"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Recursively find/replace of a string in directories and file names</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -depth -name <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>*test*<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -execdir bash -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>mv -v "$1" "${1//foo/bar}"<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> _ {} <span class="pl-cce">\;</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-recursively-find-suid-executables" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recursively-find-suid-executables"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Recursively find suid executables</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>find / <span class="pl-cce">\(</span> -perm -4000 -o -perm -2000 <span class="pl-cce">\)</span> -type f -exec ls -la {} <span class="pl-cce">\;</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-top" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-top"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Top_(software)" rel="nofollow">top</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-use-top-to-monitor-only-all-processes-with-the-specific-string" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#use-top-to-monitor-only-all-processes-with-the-specific-string"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Use top to monitor only all processes with the specific string</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>top -p <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>pgrep -d , <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>str<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>&lt;str&gt;</code> - process containing string (eg. nginx, worker)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-vmstat" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-vmstat"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Vmstat" rel="nofollow">vmstat</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-current-system-utilization-fields-in-kilobytes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-current-system-utilization-fields-in-kilobytes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show current system utilization (fields in kilobytes)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>vmstat 2 20 -t -w</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>2</code> - number of times with a defined time interval (delay)</li>
<li><code>20</code> - each execution of the command (count)</li>
<li><code>-t</code> - show timestamp</li>
<li><code>-w</code> - wide output</li>
<li><code>-S M</code> - output of the fields in megabytes instead of kilobytes</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-current-system-utilization-will-get-refreshed-every-5-seconds" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-current-system-utilization-will-get-refreshed-every-5-seconds"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show current system utilization will get refreshed every 5 seconds</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>vmstat 5 -w</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-display-report-a-summary-of-disk-operations" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#display-report-a-summary-of-disk-operations"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Display report a summary of disk operations</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>vmstat -D</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-display-report-of-event-counters-and-memory-stats" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#display-report-of-event-counters-and-memory-stats"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Display report of event counters and memory stats</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>vmstat -s</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-display-report-about-kernel-objects-stored-in-slab-layer-cache" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#display-report-about-kernel-objects-stored-in-slab-layer-cache"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Display report about kernel objects stored in slab layer cache</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>vmstat -m</pre></div>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-iostat" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-iostat"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Iostat" rel="nofollow">iostat</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-information-about-the-cpu-usage-and-io-statistics-about-all-the-partitions" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-information-about-the-cpu-usage-and-io-statistics-about-all-the-partitions"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show information about the CPU usage, and I/O statistics about all the partitions</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>iostat 2 10 -t -m</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>2</code> - number of times with a defined time interval (delay)</li>
<li><code>10</code> - each execution of the command (count)</li>
<li><code>-t</code> - show timestamp</li>
<li><code>-m</code> - fields in megabytes (<code>-k</code> - in kilobytes, default)</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-information-only-about-the-cpu-utilization" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-information-only-about-the-cpu-utilization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show information only about the CPU utilization</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>iostat 2 10 -t -m -c</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-information-only-about-the-disk-utilization" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-information-only-about-the-disk-utilization"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show information only about the disk utilization</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>iostat 2 10 -t -m -d</pre></div>

<h6><a id="user-content-track-with-child-processes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#track-with-child-processes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Track with child processes</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-track-processes-and-redirect-output-to-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#track-processes-and-redirect-output-to-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Track processes and redirect output to a file</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-track-with-print-time-spent-in-each-syscall-and-limit-length-of-print-strings" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#track-with-print-time-spent-in-each-syscall-and-limit-length-of-print-strings"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Track with print time spent in each syscall and limit length of print strings</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-compare-two-directory-trees" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#compare-two-directory-trees"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Compare two directory trees</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-highlight-the-exact-differences-based-on-characters-and-words" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#highlight-the-exact-differences-based-on-characters-and-words"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Highlight the exact differences, based on characters and words</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-compare-two-json-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#compare-two-json-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Compare two JSON files</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-compare-hex-dump" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#compare-hex-dump"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Compare Hex dump</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-en">d</span>(){ vimdiff <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;(</span>f <span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;(</span>f <span class="pl-en">$2);};f</span>(){ hexdump -C <span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-k">|</span>cut -d<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -f3-<span class="pl-k">|</span>tr -s <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span>;}<span class="pl-k">;</span> d <span class="pl-k">~</span>/bin1 <span class="pl-k">~</span>/bin2</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-diffchar" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#diffchar"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>diffchar</h6>
<p>Save <a href="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/vim-scripts/diffchar.vim/master/plugin/diffchar.vim" rel="nofollow">diffchar</a> @ <code>~/.vim/plugins</code></p>
<p>Click <code>F7</code> to switch between diff modes</p>
<p>Usefull <code>vimdiff</code> commands:</p>
<ul>
<li><code>qa</code> to exit all windows</li>
<li><code>:vertical resize 70</code> to resize window</li>
<li>set window width <code>Ctrl+W [N columns]+(Shift+)&lt;\&gt;</code></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-tail" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-tail"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tail_(Unix)" rel="nofollow">tail</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-annotate-tail--f-with-timestamps" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#annotate-tail--f-with-timestamps"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Annotate tail -f with timestamps</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tail -f file <span class="pl-k">|</span> <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">read</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date +%T.%N<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span> <span class="pl-smi">$REPLY</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-analyse-an-apache-access-log-for-the-most-common-ip-addresses" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#analyse-an-apache-access-log-for-the-most-common-ip-addresses"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Analyse an Apache access log for the most common IP addresses</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tail -10000 access_log <span class="pl-k">|</span> awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{print $1}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort <span class="pl-k">|</span> uniq -c <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort -n <span class="pl-k">|</span> tail</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-analyse-web-server-log-and-show-only-5xx-http-codes" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#analyse-web-server-log-and-show-only-5xx-http-codes"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Analyse web server log and show only 5xx http codes</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tail -n 100 -f /path/to/logfile <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HTTP/[1-2].[0-1]<span class="pl-cce">\"</span> [5]<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
