<h5><a id="user-content-tool-tar" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-tar"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tar_(computing)" rel="nofollow">tar</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-system-backup-with-exclude-specific-directories" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#system-backup-with-exclude-specific-directories"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>System backup with exclude specific directories</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> /
tar -czvpf /mnt/system<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date +%d%m%Y%s<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>.tgz --directory=/ \
--exclude=proc/<span class="pl-k">*</span> --exclude=sys/<span class="pl-k">*</span> --exclude=dev/<span class="pl-k">*</span> --exclude=mnt/<span class="pl-k">*</span> <span class="pl-c1">.</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-system-backup-with-exclude-specific-directories-pigz" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#system-backup-with-exclude-specific-directories-pigz"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>System backup with exclude specific directories (pigz)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> /
tar cvpf /backup/snapshot-<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date +%d%m%Y%s<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>.tgz --directory=/ \
--exclude=proc/<span class="pl-k">*</span> --exclude=sys/<span class="pl-k">*</span> --exclude=dev/<span class="pl-k">*</span> \
--exclude=mnt/<span class="pl-k">*</span> --exclude=tmp/<span class="pl-k">*</span> --use-compress-program=pigz <span class="pl-c1">.</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-dump" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-dump"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dump_(program)" rel="nofollow">dump</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-system-backup-to-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#system-backup-to-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>System backup to file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>dump -y -u -f /backup/system<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date +%d%m%Y%s<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>.lzo /</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-restore-system-from-lzo-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#restore-system-from-lzo-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Restore system from lzo file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">cd</span> /
restore -rf /backup/system<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date +%d%m%Y%s<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>.lzo</pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-cpulimit" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-cpulimit"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://cpulimit.sourceforge.net/" rel="nofollow">cpulimit</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-limit-the-cpu-usage-of-a-process" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#limit-the-cpu-usage-of-a-process"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Limit the cpu usage of a process</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-show-current-working-directory-of-a-process-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-current-working-directory-of-a-process-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show current working directory of a process</h6>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-taskset" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-taskset"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.cyberciti.biz/faq/taskset-cpu-affinity-command/" rel="nofollow">taskset</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-start-a-command-on-only-one-cpu-core" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#start-a-command-on-only-one-cpu-core"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Start a command on only one CPU core</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>taskset -c 0 <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>command<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span></pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-chmod" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-chmod"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Chmod" rel="nofollow">chmod</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-remove-executable-bit-from-all-files-in-the-current-directory" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-executable-bit-from-all-files-in-the-current-directory"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove executable bit from all files in the current directory</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-restore-permission-for-binchmod" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#restore-permission-for-binchmod"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Restore permission for /bin/chmod</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1:</span>
cp /bin/ls chmod.01
cp /bin/chmod chmod.01
./chmod.01 700 file

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2:</span>
/bin/busybox chmod 0700 /bin/chmod

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 3:</span>
setfacl --set u::rwx,g::---,o::--- /bin/chmod</pre></div>

<h6><a id="user-content-was-the-last-reboot-a-panic" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#was-the-last-reboot-a-panic"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Was the last reboot a panic?</h6>

grep -A1 reboot <span class="pl-k">|</span> head -2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -q shutdown <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Expected reboot<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">||</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Panic reboot<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-script" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-script"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Script_(Unix)" rel="nofollow">script</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-record-and-replay-terminal-session" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#record-and-replay-terminal-session"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Record and replay terminal session</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## Record session</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1)</span>
script -t <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>~/session.time -a <span class="pl-k">~</span>/session.log

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2)</span>
script --timing=session.time session.log

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## Replay session</span>
scriptreplay --timing=session.time session.log</pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-du" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-du"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GNU_Screen" rel="nofollow">du</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-20-biggest-directories-with-k-m-g" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-20-biggest-directories-with-k-m-g"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show 20 biggest directories with 'K M G'</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>du <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sort -r -n <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{split("K M G",v); s=1; while($1&gt;1024){$1/=1024; s++} print int($1)" "v[s]"\t"$2}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
head -n 20</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-inotifywait" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-inotifywait"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/GNU_Screen" rel="nofollow">inotifywait</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-init-tool-everytime-a-file-in-a-directory-is-modified" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#init-tool-everytime-a-file-in-a-directory-is-modified"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Init tool everytime a file in a directory is modified</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> inotifywait -r -e MODIFY dir/ <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> ls dir/ <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span><span class="pl-k">;</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-openssl" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-openssl"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.openssl.org/" rel="nofollow">openssl</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-connection-to-the-remote-host" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-connection-to-the-remote-host"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing connection to the remote host</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> openssl s_client -connect google.com:443 -showcerts</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-debug-mode" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-debug-mode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing connection to the remote host (debug mode)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> openssl s_client -connect google.com:443 -showcerts -tlsextdebug -status</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-with-sni-support" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-with-sni-support"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing connection to the remote host (with SNI support)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> openssl s_client -showcerts -servername google.com -connect google.com:443</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-with-specific-ssl-version" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-with-specific-ssl-version"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing connection to the remote host with specific ssl version</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>openssl s_client -tls1_2 -connect google.com:443</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-with-specific-ssl-cipher" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-connection-to-the-remote-host-with-specific-ssl-cipher"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing connection to the remote host with specific ssl cipher</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>openssl s_client -cipher <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>AES128-SHA<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -connect google.com:443</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-verify-0-rtt" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#verify-0-rtt"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Verify 0-RTT</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>_host=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>example.com<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

cat <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> req.in <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">HEAD / HTTP/1.1</span>
<span class="pl-s">Host: $_host</span>
<span class="pl-s">Connection: close</span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span>

openssl s_client -connect <span class="pl-smi">${_host}</span>:443 -tls1_3 -sess_out session.pem -ign_eof <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> req.in
openssl s_client -connect <span class="pl-smi">${_host}</span>:443 -tls1_3 -sess_in session.pem -early_data req.in</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-private-key-without-passphrase" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-private-key-without-passphrase"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate private key without passphrase</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _len: 2048, 4096</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _len=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4096<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl genrsa -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> <span class="pl-smi">${_len}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-private-key-with-passphrase" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-private-key-with-passphrase"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate private key with passphrase</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _ciph: des3, aes128, aes256</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _len: 2048, 4096</span>
( _ciph=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>aes128<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _len=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4096<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl genrsa -<span class="pl-smi">${_ciph}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> <span class="pl-smi">${_len}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-remove-passphrase-from-private-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-passphrase-from-private-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove passphrase from private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_unp=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private_unp.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl rsa -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_unp}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-encrypt-existing-private-key-with-a-passphrase" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#encrypt-existing-private-key-with-a-passphrase"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Encrypt existing private key with a passphrase</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _ciph: des3, aes128, aes256</span>
( _ciph=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>aes128<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_pass=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private_pass.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl rsa -<span class="pl-smi">${_ciph}</span> -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pass}</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-check-private-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#check-private-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Check private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl rsa -check -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-get-public-key-from-private-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#get-public-key-from-private-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Get public key from private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_pub=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>public.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl rsa -pubout -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pub}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-private-key-and-csr" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-private-key-and-csr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate private key and CSR</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_csr=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>request.csr<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _len=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4096<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_csr}</span> -new -newkey rsa:<span class="pl-smi">${_len}</span> -nodes -keyout <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-csr" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-csr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate CSR</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_csr=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>request.csr<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_csr}</span> -new -key <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-csr-metadata-from-existing-certificate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-csr-metadata-from-existing-certificate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate CSR (metadata from existing certificate)</h6>
<blockquote>
<p>Where <code>private.key</code> is the existing private key. As you can see you do not generate this CSR from your certificate (public key). Also you do not generate the "same" CSR, just a new one to request a new certificate.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_csr=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>request.csr<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_crt=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cert.crt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl x509 -x509toreq -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_crt}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_csr}</span> -signkey <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-csr-with--config-param" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-csr-with--config-param"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate CSR with -config param</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_csr=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>request.csr<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -new -sha256 -key <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_csr}</span> \
-config <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">&lt;(</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">cat <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">[req]</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">default_bits        = 2048</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">default_md          = sha256</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">prompt              = no</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">distinguished_name  = dn</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">req_extensions      = req_ext</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s"></span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">[ dn ]</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">C   = "&lt;two-letter ISO abbreviation for your country&gt;"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">ST  = "&lt;state or province where your organisation is legally located&gt;"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">L   = "&lt;city where your organisation is legally located&gt;"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">O   = "&lt;legal name of your organisation&gt;"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">OU  = "&lt;section of the organisation&gt;"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">CN  = "&lt;fully qualified domain name&gt;"</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s"></span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">[ req_ext ]</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">subjectAltName = @alt_names</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s"></span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">[ alt_names ]</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">DNS.1 = &lt;fully qualified domain name&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">DNS.2 = &lt;next domain&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s">DNS.3 = &lt;next domain&gt;</span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span></span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>)</pre></div>
<p>Other values in <code>[ dn ]</code>:</p>
<blockquote>
<p>Look at this great explanation: <a href="https://apfelboymchen.net/gnu/notes/openssl%20multidomain%20with%20config%20files.html" rel="nofollow">How to create multidomain certificates using config files</a></p>
</blockquote>
<pre><code>countryName            = "DE"                     # C=
stateOrProvinceName    = "Hessen"                 # ST=
localityName           = "Keller"                 # L=
postalCode             = "424242"                 # L/postalcode=
streetAddress          = "Crater 1621"            # L/street=
organizationName       = "apfelboymschule"        # O=
organizationalUnitName = "IT Department"          # OU=
commonName             = "example.com"            # CN=
emailAddress           = "webmaster@example.com"  # CN/emailAddress=
</code></pre>
<h6><a id="user-content-list-available-ec-curves" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#list-available-ec-curves"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>List available EC curves</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>openssl ecparam -list_curves</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-ecdsa-private-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-ecdsa-private-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate ECDSA private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _curve: prime256v1, secp521r1, secp384r1</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _curve=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>prime256v1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl ecparam -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -name <span class="pl-smi">${_curve}</span> -genkey )

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _curve: X25519</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _curve=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>x25519<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl genpkey -algorithm <span class="pl-smi">${_curve}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-ecdsa-private-and-public-keys" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-ecdsa-private-and-public-keys"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print ECDSA private and public keys</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl ec -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -noout -text )

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> For x25519 only extracting public key</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_pub=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>public.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl pkey -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -pubout -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pub}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-private-key-with-csr-ecc" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-private-key-with-csr-ecc"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate private key with CSR (ECC)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _curve: prime256v1, secp521r1, secp384r1</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.com.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_csr=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.com.csr<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _curve=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>prime256v1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl ecparam -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -name <span class="pl-smi">${_curve}</span> -genkey <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -new -key <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_csr}</span> -sha256 )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-self-signed-certificate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-self-signed-certificate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate self-signed certificate</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _len: 2048, 4096</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_out=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.crt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _len=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>4096<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _days=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>365<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -newkey rsa:<span class="pl-smi">${_len}</span> -nodes \
-keyout <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -x509 -days <span class="pl-smi">${_days}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_out}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-self-signed-certificate-from-existing-private-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-self-signed-certificate-from-existing-private-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate self-signed certificate from existing private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _len: 2048, 4096</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_out=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.crt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _days=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>365<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -key <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -nodes \
-x509 -days <span class="pl-smi">${_days}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_out}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-self-signed-certificate-from-existing-private-key-and-csr" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-self-signed-certificate-from-existing-private-key-and-csr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate self-signed certificate from existing private key and csr</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> _len: 2048, 4096</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_csr=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.csr<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_out=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>domain.crt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _days=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>365<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl x509 -signkey <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> -nodes \
-in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_csr}</span> -req -days <span class="pl-smi">${_days}</span> -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_out}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-dh-public-parameters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-dh-public-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate DH public parameters</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _dh_size=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>2048<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl dhparam -out /etc/nginx/ssl/dhparam_<span class="pl-smi">${_dh_size}</span>.pem <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_dh_size</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-display-dh-public-parameters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#display-dh-public-parameters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Display DH public parameters</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>openssl pkeyparam -in dhparam.pem -text</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-extract-private-key-from-pfx" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#extract-private-key-from-pfx"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Extract private key from pfx</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd_pfx=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cert.pfx<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_key=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>key.pem<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl pkcs12 -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pfx}</span> -nocerts -nodes -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_key}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-extract-private-key-and-certs-from-pfx" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#extract-private-key-and-certs-from-pfx"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Extract private key and certs from pfx</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd_pfx=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cert.pfx<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_pem=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>key_certs.pem<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl pkcs12 -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pfx}</span> -nodes -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pem}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-convert-der-to-pem" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#convert-der-to-pem"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Convert DER to PEM</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd_der=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cert.crt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_pem=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cert.pem<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl x509 -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_der}</span> -inform der -outform pem -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pem}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-convert-pem-to-der" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#convert-pem-to-der"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Convert PEM to DER</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd_der=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cert.crt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> _fd_pem=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>cert.pem<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl x509 -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_pem}</span> -outform der -out <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_der}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-verification-of-the-private-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#verification-of-the-private-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Verification of the private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl rsa -noout -text -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-verification-of-the-public-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#verification-of-the-public-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Verification of the public key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1)</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>public.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl pkey -noout -text -pubin -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2)</span>
( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>private.key<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl rsa -inform PEM -noout -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> <span class="pl-k">&amp;</span><span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> /dev/null <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
<span class="pl-k">if</span> [ <span class="pl-smi">$?</span> <span class="pl-k">=</span> 0 ] <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> -en <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>OK\n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">fi</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-verification-of-the-certificate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#verification-of-the-certificate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Verification of the certificate</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>certificate.crt<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> format: pem, cer, crt \</span>
openssl x509 -noout -text -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-verification-of-the-csr" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#verification-of-the-csr"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Verification of the CSR</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>( _fd_csr=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>request.csr<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -text -noout -in <span class="pl-smi">${_fd_csr}</span> )</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-check-whether-the-private-key-and-the-certificate-match" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#check-whether-the-private-key-and-the-certificate-match"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Check whether the private key and the certificate match</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>(openssl rsa -noout -modulus -in private.key <span class="pl-k">|</span> openssl md5 <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl x509 -noout -modulus -in certificate.crt <span class="pl-k">|</span> openssl md5) <span class="pl-k">|</span> uniq</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-check-whether-the-private-key-and-the-csr-match" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#check-whether-the-private-key-and-the-csr-match"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Check whether the private key and the CSR match</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>(openssl rsa -noout -modulus -in private.key <span class="pl-k">|</span> openssl md5 <span class="pl-k">;</span> \
openssl req -noout -modulus -in request.csr <span class="pl-k">|</span> openssl md5) <span class="pl-k">|</span> uniq</pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-secure-delete" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-secure-delete"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://wiki.archlinux.org/index.php/Securely_wipe_disk" rel="nofollow">secure-delete</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-secure-delete-with-shred" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#secure-delete-with-shred"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Secure delete with shred</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>shred -vfuz -n 10 file
shred --verbose --random-source=/dev/urandom -n 1 /dev/sda</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-secure-delete-with-scrub" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#secure-delete-with-scrub"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Secure delete with scrub</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>scrub -p dod /dev/sda
scrub -p dod -r file</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-secure-delete-with-badblocks" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#secure-delete-with-badblocks"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Secure delete with badblocks</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>badblocks -s -w -t random -v /dev/sda
badblocks -c 10240 -s -w -t random -v /dev/sda</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-secure-delete-with-secure-delete" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#secure-delete-with-secure-delete"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Secure delete with secure-delete</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>srm -vz /tmp/file
sfill -vz /local
sdmem -v
swapoff /dev/sda5 <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> sswap -vz /dev/sda5</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-dd" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-dd"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dd_(Unix)" rel="nofollow">dd</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-dd-status-every-so-often" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-dd-status-every-so-often"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show dd status every so often</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>dd <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>dd_params<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> status=progress
watch --interval 5 killall -USR1 dd</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-redirect-output-to-a-file-with-dd" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#redirect-output-to-a-file-with-dd"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Redirect output to a file with dd</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>string<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> dd of=filename</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-gpg" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-gpg"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.gnupg.org/" rel="nofollow">gpg</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-export-public-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#export-public-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Export public key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>gpg --export --armor <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>&lt;username&gt;<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> username.pkey</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>--export</code> - export all keys from all keyrings or specific key</li>
<li><code>-a|--armor</code> - create ASCII armored output</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-encrypt-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#encrypt-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Encrypt file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>gpg -e -r <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>&lt;username&gt;<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> dump.sql</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-e|--encrypt</code> - encrypt data</li>
<li><code>-r|--recipient</code> - encrypt for specific </li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-decrypt-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#decrypt-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Decrypt file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>gpg -o dump.sql -d dump.sql.gpg</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-o|--output</code> - use as output file</li>
<li><code>-d|--decrypt</code> - decrypt data (default)</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-search-recipient" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#search-recipient"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Search recipient</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>gpg --keyserver hkp://keyserver.ubuntu.com --search-keys <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>&lt;username&gt;<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>--keyserver</code> - set specific key server</li>
<li><code>--search-keys</code> - search for keys on a key server</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-list-all-of-the-packets-in-an-encrypted-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#list-all-of-the-packets-in-an-encrypted-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>List all of the packets in an encrypted file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>gpg --batch --list-packets archive.gpg
gpg2 --batch --list-packets archive.gpg</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-system-other" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-system-other"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://github.com/trimstray/the-book-of-secret-knowledge#tool-system-other">system-other</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-reboot-system-from-init" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#reboot-system-from-init"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Reboot system from init</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">exec</span> /sbin/init 6</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-init-system-from-single-user-mode" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#init-system-from-single-user-mode"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Init system from single user mode</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">exec</span> /sbin/init</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-current-working-directory-of-a-process-2" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-current-working-directory-of-a-process-2"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show current working directory of a process</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>readlink -f /proc/<span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>PID<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>/cwd</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-actual-pathname-of-the-executed-command" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-actual-pathname-of-the-executed-command"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show actual pathname of the executed command</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>readlink -f /proc/<span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>PID<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>/exe</pre></div>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-curl" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-curl"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://curl.haxx.se" rel="nofollow">curl</a></h5>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>curl -Iks https://www.google.com</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-I</code> - show response headers only</li>
<li><code>-k</code> - insecure connection when using ssl</li>
<li><code>-s</code> - silent mode (not display body)</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>curl -Iks --location -X GET -A <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>x-agent<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> https://www.google.com</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>--location</code> - follow redirects</li>
<li><code>-X</code> - set method</li>
<li><code>-A</code> - set user-agent</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>curl -Iks --location -X GET -A <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>x-agent<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> --proxy http://127.0.0.1:16379 https://www.google.com</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>--proxy [socks5://|http://]</code> - set proxy server</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>curl -o file.pdf -C - https://example.com/Aiju2goo0Ja2.pdf</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-o</code> - write output to file</li>
<li><code>-C</code> - resume the transfer</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-find-your-external-ip-address-external-services" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#find-your-external-ip-address-external-services"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Find your external IP address (external services)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>curl ipinfo.io
curl ipinfo.io/ip
curl icanhazip.com
curl ifconfig.me/ip <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span></pre></div>
