<h6><a id="user-content-repeat-url-request" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#repeat-url-request"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Repeat URL request</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> URL sequence substitution with a dummy query string:</span>
curl -ks https://example.com/<span class="pl-k">?</span>[1-20]

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> With shell 'for' loop:</span>
<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">i</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> {1..20} <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> curl -ks https://example.com/ <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-check-dns-and-http-trace-with-headers-for-specific-domains" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#check-dns-and-http-trace-with-headers-for-specific-domains"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Check DNS and HTTP trace with headers for specific domains</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## Set domains and external dns servers.</span>
_domain_list=(google.com) <span class="pl-k">;</span> _dns_list=(<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>8.8.8.8<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1.1.1.1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>)

<span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">_domain</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${_domain_list[@]}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>

  <span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>=%.0s<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> {1..48}

  <span class="pl-c1">echo</span>

  <span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>[<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>e[1;32m+<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>e[m] resolve: %s<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_domain</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">_dns</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${_dns_list[@]}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Resolve domain.</span>
    host <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${_domain}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${_dns}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

    <span class="pl-c1">echo</span>

  <span class="pl-k">done</span>

  <span class="pl-k">for</span> <span class="pl-smi">_proto</span> <span class="pl-k">in</span> http https <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span>

    <span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>[<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>e[1;32m+<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>e[m] trace + headers: %s://%s<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_proto</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_domain</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

    <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Get trace and http headers.</span>
    curl -Iks -A <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>x-agent<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> --location <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${_proto}</span>://<span class="pl-smi">${_domain}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

    <span class="pl-c1">echo</span>

  <span class="pl-k">done</span>

<span class="pl-k">done</span>

<span class="pl-c1">unset</span> _domain_list _dns_list</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-httpie" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-httpie"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://httpie.org/" rel="nofollow">httpie</a></h5>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>http -p Hh https://www.google.com</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-p</code> - print request and response headers
<ul>
<li><code>H</code> - request headers</li>
<li><code>B</code> - request body</li>
<li><code>h</code> - response headers</li>
<li><code>b</code> - response body</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>http -p Hh https://www.google.com --follow --verify no</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-F, --follow</code> - follow redirects</li>
<li><code>--verify no</code> - skip SSL verification</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>http -p Hh https://www.google.com --follow --verify no \
--proxy http:http://127.0.0.1:16379</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>--proxy [http:]</code> - set proxy server</li>
</ul>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-ssh" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-ssh"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.openssh.com/" rel="nofollow">ssh</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-escape-sequence" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#escape-sequence"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Escape Sequence</h6>
<pre><code># Supported escape sequences:
~.  - terminate connection (and any multiplexed sessions)
~B  - send a BREAK to the remote system
~C  - open a command line
~R  - Request rekey (SSH protocol 2 only)
~^Z - suspend ssh
~#  - list forwarded connections
~&amp;  - background ssh (when waiting for connections to terminate)
~?  - this message
~~  - send the escape character by typing it twice
</code></pre>
<h6><a id="user-content-compare-a-remote-file-with-a-local-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#compare-a-remote-file-with-a-local-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Compare a remote file with a local file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ssh user@host cat /path/to/remotefile <span class="pl-k">|</span> diff /path/to/localfile -</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-ssh-connection-through-host-in-the-middle" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ssh-connection-through-host-in-the-middle"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>SSH connection through host in the middle</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ssh -t reachable_host ssh unreachable_host</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-run-command-over-ssh-on-remote-host" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#run-command-over-ssh-on-remote-host"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Run command over SSH on remote host</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>cat <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> cmd.txt <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">cat /etc/hosts</span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span>

ssh host -l user <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span><span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>cmd.txt<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-get-public-key-from-private-key-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#get-public-key-from-private-key-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Get public key from private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ssh-keygen -y -f <span class="pl-k">~</span>/.ssh/id_rsa</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-get-all-fingerprints" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#get-all-fingerprints"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Get all fingerprints</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ssh-keygen -l -f .ssh/known_hosts</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-ssh-authentication-with-user-password" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ssh-authentication-with-user-password"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>SSH authentication with user password</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ssh -o PreferredAuthentications=password -o PubkeyAuthentication=no user@remote_host</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-ssh-authentication-with-publickey" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ssh-authentication-with-publickey"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>SSH authentication with publickey</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ssh -o PreferredAuthentications=publickey -o PubkeyAuthentication=yes -i id_rsa user@remote_host</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-simple-recording-ssh-session" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#simple-recording-ssh-session"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Simple recording SSH session</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">_ssh_sesslog()</span> {

  _sesdir=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>&lt;path/to/session/logs&gt;<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  mkdir -p <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${_sesdir}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> \
  ssh <span class="pl-smi">$@</span> <span class="pl-k">2&gt;&amp;1</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> tee -a <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">${_sesdir}</span>/<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date +%Y%m%d<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>.log<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Alias:</span>
<span class="pl-c1">alias</span> ssh=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>_ssh_sesslog<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-using-keychain-for-ssh-logins" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#using-keychain-for-ssh-logins"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Using Keychain for SSH logins</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## Delete all of ssh-agent's keys.</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">_scl()</span> {

  /usr/bin/keychain --clear

}

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## Add key to keychain.</span>
<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">_scg()</span> {

  /usr/bin/keychain /path/to/private-key
  <span class="pl-c1">source</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$HOME</span>/.keychain/<span class="pl-smi">$HOSTNAME</span>-sh<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

}</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-ssh-login-without-processing-any-login-scripts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ssh-login-without-processing-any-login-scripts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>SSH login without processing any login scripts</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ssh -tt user@host bash</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-ssh-local-port-forwarding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ssh-local-port-forwarding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>SSH local port forwarding</h6>
<p>Example 1:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Forwarding our local 2250 port to nmap.org:443 from localhost through localhost</span>
host<span class="pl-k">1&gt;</span> ssh -L 2250:nmap.org:443 localhost

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Connect to the service:</span>
host<span class="pl-k">1&gt;</span> curl -Iks --location -X GET https://localhost:2250</pre></div>
<p>Example 2:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Forwarding our local 9051 port to db.d.x:5432 from localhost through node.d.y</span>
host<span class="pl-k">1&gt;</span> ssh -nNT -L 9051:db.d.x:5432 node.d.y

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Connect to the service:</span>
host<span class="pl-k">1&gt;</span> psql -U db_user -d db_dev -p 9051 -h localhost</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-n</code> - redirects stdin from <code>/dev/null</code></li>
<li><code>-N</code> - do not execute a remote command</li>
<li><code>-T</code> - disable pseudo-terminal allocation</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-ssh-remote-port-forwarding" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ssh-remote-port-forwarding"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>SSH remote port forwarding</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Forwarding our local 9051 port to db.d.x:5432 from host2 through node.d.y</span>
host<span class="pl-k">1&gt;</span> ssh -nNT -R 9051:db.d.x:5432 node.d.y

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Connect to the service:</span>
host<span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span> psql -U postgres -d postgres -p 8000 -h localhost</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-linux-dev" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-linux-dev"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.tldp.org/LDP/abs/html/devref1.html" rel="nofollow">linux-dev</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-remote-connection-to-port" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-remote-connection-to-port"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing remote connection to port</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>timeout 1 bash -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>&lt;/dev/&lt;proto&gt;/&lt;host&gt;/&lt;port&gt;<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>/dev/null <span class="pl-k">2&gt;&amp;1</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> <span class="pl-smi">$?</span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>&lt;proto</code> - set protocol (tcp/udp)</li>
<li><code>&lt;host&gt;</code> - set remote host</li>
<li><code>&lt;port&gt;</code> - set destination port</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-read-and-write-to-tcp-or-udp-sockets-with-common-bash-tools" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#read-and-write-to-tcp-or-udp-sockets-with-common-bash-tools"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Read and write to TCP or UDP sockets with common bash tools</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c1">exec</span> <span class="pl-k">5&lt;&gt;</span>/dev/tcp/<span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>host<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span>/<span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>port<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> cat <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-k">&amp;</span>5 <span class="pl-k">&amp;</span> cat <span class="pl-k">&gt;&amp;5</span><span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-c1">exec</span> <span class="pl-k">5&gt;&amp;</span>-</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-tcpdump" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-tcpdump"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://www.tcpdump.org/" rel="nofollow">tcpdump</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-filter-incoming-on-interface-traffic-specific-ipport" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#filter-incoming-on-interface-traffic-specific-ipport"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Filter incoming (on interface) traffic (specific ip:port)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -ne -i eth0 -Q <span class="pl-k">in</span> host 192.168.252.1 and port 443</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-n</code> - don't convert addresses (<code>-nn</code> will not resolve hostnames or ports)</li>
<li><code>-e</code> - print the link-level headers</li>
<li><code>-i [iface|any]</code> - set interface</li>
<li><code>-Q|-D [in|out|inout]</code> - choose send/receive direction (<code>-D</code> - for old tcpdump versions)</li>
<li><code>host [ip|hostname]</code> - set host, also <code>[host not]</code></li>
<li><code>[and|or]</code> - set logic</li>
<li><code>port [1-65535]</code> - set port number, also <code>[port not]</code></li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-filter-incoming-on-interface-traffic-specific-ipport-and-write-to-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#filter-incoming-on-interface-traffic-specific-ipport-and-write-to-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Filter incoming (on interface) traffic (specific ip:port) and write to a file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -ne -i eth0 -Q <span class="pl-k">in</span> host 192.168.252.1 and port 443 -c 5 -w tcpdump.pcap</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-c [num]</code> - capture only num number of packets</li>
<li><code>-w [filename]</code> - write packets to file, <code>-r [filename]</code> - reading from file</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-capture-all-icmp-packets" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#capture-all-icmp-packets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Capture all ICMP packets</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -nei eth0 icmp</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-check-protocol-used-tcp-or-udp-for-service" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#check-protocol-used-tcp-or-udp-for-service"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Check protocol used (TCP or UDP) for service</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -nei eth0 tcp port 22 -vv -X <span class="pl-k">|</span> egrep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>TCP|UDP<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-display-ascii-text-to-parse-the-output-using-grep-or-other" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#display-ascii-text-to-parse-the-output-using-grep-or-other"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Display ASCII text (to parse the output using grep or other)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -i eth0 -A -s0 port 443</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-grab-everything-between-two-keywords" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#grab-everything-between-two-keywords"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Grab everything between two keywords</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -i eth0 port 80 -X <span class="pl-k">|</span> sed -n -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/username/,/=ldap/ p<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-grab-user-and-pass-ever-plain-http" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#grab-user-and-pass-ever-plain-http"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Grab user and pass ever plain http</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -i eth0  port http -l -A <span class="pl-k">|</span> egrep -i \
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>pass=|pwd=|log=|login=|user=|username=|pw=|passw=|passwd=|password=|pass:|user:|username:|password:|login:|pass |user <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
--color=auto --line-buffered -B20</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-extract-http-user-agent-from-http-request-header" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#extract-http-user-agent-from-http-request-header"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Extract HTTP User Agent from HTTP request header</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -ei eth0 -nn -A -s1500 -l <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>User-Agent:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-capture-only-http-get-and-post-packets" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#capture-only-http-get-and-post-packets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Capture only HTTP GET and POST packets</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -ei eth0 -s 0 -A -vv \
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>tcp[((tcp[12:1] &amp; 0xf0) &gt;&gt; 2):4] = 0x47455420<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> or <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>tcp[((tcp[12:1] &amp; 0xf0) &gt;&gt; 2):4] = 0x504f5354<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<p>or simply:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -ei eth0 -s 0 -v -n -l <span class="pl-k">|</span> egrep -i <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>POST /|GET /|Host:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-rotate-capture-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rotate-capture-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Rotate capture files</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -ei eth0 -w /tmp/capture-%H.pcap -G 3600 -C 200</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-G &lt;num&gt;</code> - pcap will be created every <code>&lt;num&gt;</code> seconds</li>
<li><code>-C &lt;size&gt;</code> - close the current pcap and open a new one if is larger than <code>&lt;size&gt;</code></li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-top-hosts-by-packets" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#top-hosts-by-packets"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Top hosts by packets</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -ei enp0s25 -nnn -t -c 200 <span class="pl-k">|</span> cut -f 1,2,3,4 -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>.<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort <span class="pl-k">|</span> uniq -c <span class="pl-k">|</span> sort -nr <span class="pl-k">|</span> head -n 20</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-excludes-any-rfc-1918-private-address" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#excludes-any-rfc-1918-private-address"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Excludes any RFC 1918 private address</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>tcpdump -nei eth0 <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>not (src net (10 or 172.16/12 or 192.168/16) and dst net (10 or 172.16/12 or 192.168/16))<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-tcpick" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-tcpick"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://tcpick.sourceforge.net/" rel="nofollow">tcpick</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-analyse-packets-in-real-time" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#analyse-packets-in-real-time"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Analyse packets in real-time</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> tcpick -a -C -r dump.pcap <span class="pl-k">;</span> sleep 2 <span class="pl-k">;</span> clear <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-ngrep" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-ngrep"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://ngrep.sourceforge.net/usage.html" rel="nofollow">ngrep</a></h5>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ngrep -d eth0 <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>www.domain.com<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> port 443</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-d [iface|any]</code> - set interface</li>
<li><code>[domain]</code> - set hostname</li>
<li><code>port [1-65535]</code> - set port number</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ngrep -d eth0 <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>www.domain.com<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> src host 10.240.20.2 and port 443</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>(host [ip|hostname])</code> - filter by ip or hostname</li>
<li><code>(port [1-65535])</code> - filter by port number</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ngrep -d eth0 -qt -O ngrep.pcap <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>www.domain.com<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> port 443</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-q</code> - quiet mode (only payloads)</li>
<li><code>-t</code> - added timestamps</li>
<li><code>-O [filename]</code> - save output to file, <code>-I [filename]</code> - reading from file</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ngrep -d eth0 -qt <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>HTTP<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>tcp<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>HTTP</code> - show http headers</li>
<li><code>tcp|udp</code> - set protocol</li>
<li><code>[src|dst] host [ip|hostname]</code> - set direction for specific node</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>ngrep -l -q -d eth0 -i <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>User-Agent: curl*<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-l</code> - stdout line buffered</li>
<li><code>-i</code> - case-insensitive search</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-hping3" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-hping3"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://www.hping.org/" rel="nofollow">hping3</a></h5>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>hping3 -V -p 80 -s 5050 <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>scan_type<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> www.google.com</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-V|--verbose</code> - verbose mode</li>
<li><code>-p|--destport</code> - set destination port</li>
<li><code>-s|--baseport</code> - set source port</li>
<li><code>&lt;scan_type&gt;</code> - set scan type
<ul>
<li><code>-F|--fin</code> - set FIN flag, port open if no reply</li>
<li><code>-S|--syn</code> - set SYN flag</li>
<li><code>-P|--push</code> - set PUSH flag</li>
<li><code>-A|--ack</code> - set ACK flag (use when ping is blocked, RST response back if the port is open)</li>
<li><code>-U|--urg</code> - set URG flag</li>
<li><code>-Y|--ymas</code> - set Y unused flag (0x80 - nullscan), port open if no reply</li>
<li><code>-M 0 -UPF</code> - set TCP sequence number and scan type (URG+PUSH+FIN), port open if no reply</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>hping3 -V -c 1 -1 -C 8 www.google.com</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-c [num]</code> - packet count</li>
<li><code>-1</code> - set ICMP mode</li>
<li><code>-C|--icmptype [icmp-num]</code> - set icmp type (default icmp-echo = 8)</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>hping3 -V -c 1000000 -d 120 -S -w 64 -p 80 --flood --rand-source <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>remote_host<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>--flood</code> - sent packets as fast as possible (don't show replies)</li>
<li><code>--rand-source</code> - random source address mode</li>
<li><code>-d --data</code> - data size</li>
<li><code>-w|--win</code> - winsize (default 64)</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-nmap" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-nmap"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://nmap.org/" rel="nofollow">nmap</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-ping-scans-the-network" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#ping-scans-the-network"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Ping scans the network</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nmap -sP 192.168.0.0/24</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-only-open-ports" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-only-open-ports"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show only open ports</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nmap -F --open 192.168.0.0/24</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-full-tcp-port-scan-using-with-service-version-detection" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#full-tcp-port-scan-using-with-service-version-detection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Full TCP port scan using with service version detection</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nmap -p 1-65535 -sV -sS -T4 192.168.0.0/24</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-nmap-scan-and-pass-output-to-nikto" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#nmap-scan-and-pass-output-to-nikto"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Nmap scan and pass output to Nikto</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nmap -p80,443 192.168.0.0/24 -oG - <span class="pl-k">|</span> nikto.pl -h -</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-recon-specific-ipservice-with-nmap-nse-scripts-stack" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#recon-specific-ipservice-with-nmap-nse-scripts-stack"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Recon specific ip:service with Nmap NSE scripts stack</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Set variables:</span>
_hosts=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>192.168.250.10<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
_ports=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>80,443<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Set Nmap NSE scripts stack:</span>
_nmap_nse_scripts=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>+dns-brute,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-auth-finder,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-chrono,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-cookie-flags,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-cors,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-cross-domain-policy,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-csrf,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-dombased-xss,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-enum,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-errors,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-git,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-grep,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-internal-ip-disclosure,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-jsonp-detection,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-malware-host,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-methods,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-passwd,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-phpself-xss,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-php-version,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-robots.txt,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-sitemap-generator,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-shellshock,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-stored-xss,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-title,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-unsafe-output-escaping,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-useragent-tester,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-vhosts,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-waf-detect,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-waf-fingerprint,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +http-xssed,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +traceroute-geolocation.nse,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +ssl-enum-ciphers,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +whois-domain,<span class="pl-cce">\</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">                   +whois-ip<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Set Nmap NSE script params:</span>
_nmap_nse_scripts_args=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>dns-brute.domain=<span class="pl-smi">${_hosts}</span>,http-cross-domain-policy.domain-lookup=true,<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
_nmap_nse_scripts_args+=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http-waf-detect.aggro,http-waf-detect.detectBodyChanges,<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
_nmap_nse_scripts_args+=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http-waf-fingerprint.intensive=1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Perform scan:</span>
nmap --script=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_nmap_nse_scripts</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> --script-args=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_nmap_nse_scripts_args</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -p <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_ports</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_hosts</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-netcat" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-netcat"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://netcat.sourceforge.net/" rel="nofollow">netcat</a></h5>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nc -kl 5000</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-l</code> - listen for an incoming connection</li>
<li><code>-k</code> - listening after client has disconnected</li>
<li><code>&gt;filename.out</code> - save receive data to file (optional)</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nc 192.168.0.1 5051 <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> filename.in</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>&lt; filename.in</code> - send data to remote host</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nc -vz 10.240.30.3 5000</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-v</code> - verbose output</li>
<li><code>-z</code> - scan for listening daemons</li>
</ul>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>nc -vzu 10.240.30.3 1-65535</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-u</code> - scan only udp ports</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-transfer-data-file-archive" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#transfer-data-file-archive"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Transfer data file (archive)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>server<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> nc -l 5000 <span class="pl-k">|</span> tar xzvfp -
client<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> tar czvfp - /path/to/dir <span class="pl-k">|</span> nc 10.240.30.3 5000</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-launch-remote-shell" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#launch-remote-shell"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Launch remote shell</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1)</span>
server<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> nc -l 5000 -e /bin/bash
client<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> nc 10.240.30.3 5000

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2)</span>
server<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> rm -f /tmp/f<span class="pl-k">;</span> mkfifo /tmp/f
server<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> cat /tmp/f <span class="pl-k">|</span> /bin/bash -i <span class="pl-k">2&gt;&amp;1</span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> nc -l 127.0.0.1 5000 <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> /tmp/f
client<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> nc 10.240.30.3 5000</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-simple-file-server" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#simple-file-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Simple file server</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> nc -l 5000 <span class="pl-k">|</span> tar -xvf - <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-simple-minimal-http-server" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#simple-minimal-http-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Simple minimal HTTP Server</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">true</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> nc -l -p 1500 -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>echo -e "HTTP/1.1 200 OK\n\n $(date)"<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-simple-http-server" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#simple-http-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Simple HTTP Server</h6>
<blockquote>
<p>Restarts web server after each request - remove <code>while</code> condition for only single connection.</p>
</blockquote>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>cat <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> index.html <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span>
<span class="pl-s">&lt;!doctype html&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;head&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">        &lt;meta charset="utf-8"&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">        &lt;meta http-equiv="X-UA-Compatible" content="IE=edge,chrome=1"&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">        &lt;title&gt;&lt;/title&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">        &lt;meta name="description" content=""&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">        &lt;meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1"&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;/head&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;body&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;p&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">      Hello! It's a site.</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;/p&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">    &lt;/body&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s">&lt;/html&gt;</span>
<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-k">__EOF__</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>server<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> <span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">:</span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> \
(echo -ne <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>HTTP/1.1 200 OK\r\nContent-Length: <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>wc -c <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>index.html<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>\r\n\r\n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> cat index.html<span class="pl-k">;</span>) <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
nc -l -p 5000 \
<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span></pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-p</code> - port number</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-simple-http-proxy-single-connection" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#simple-http-proxy-single-connection"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Simple HTTP Proxy (single connection)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#!</span>/usr/bin/env bash</span>

<span class="pl-k">if</span> [[ <span class="pl-smi">$#</span> <span class="pl-k">!=</span> 2 ]] <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>
  <span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>%s<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
         <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>usage: ./nc-proxy listen-port bk_host:bk_port<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
<span class="pl-k">fi</span>

_listen_port=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
_bk_host=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>echo <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$2</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> cut -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -f1<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>
_bk_port=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>echo <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$2</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> cut -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -f2<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>

<span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>  lport: %s<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>nbk_host: %s<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>nbk_port: %s<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> \
       <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_listen_port</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_bk_host</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_bk_port</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

_tmp=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>mktemp -d<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>
_back=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_tmp</span>/pipe.back<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
_sent=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_tmp</span>/pipe.sent<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
_recv=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_tmp</span>/pipe.recv<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c1">trap</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>rm -rf "$_tmp"<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> EXIT

mkfifo -m 0600 <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_back</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_sent</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_recv</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

sed <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>s/^/=&gt; /<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_sent</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&amp;</span>
sed <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>s/^/&lt;=  /<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_recv</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&amp;</span>

nc -l -p <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_listen_port</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_back</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
tee <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_sent</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
nc <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_bk_host</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_bk_port</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
tee <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_recv</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_back</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>server<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> chmod +x nc-proxy <span class="pl-k">&amp;&amp;</span> ./nc-proxy 8080 192.168.252.10:8000
  lport: 8080
bk_host: 192.168.252.10
bk_port: 8000

client<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> http -p h 10.240.30.3:8080
HTTP/1.1 200 OK
Accept-Ranges: bytes
Cache-Control: max-age=31536000
Content-Length: 2748
Content-Type: text/html<span class="pl-k">;</span> charset=utf-8
Date: Sun, 01 Jul 2018 20:12:08 GMT
Last-Modified: Sun, 01 Apr 2018 21:53:37 GMT</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-create-a-single-use-tcp-or-udp-proxy" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#create-a-single-use-tcp-or-udp-proxy"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Create a single-use TCP or UDP proxy</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## TCP -&gt; TCP</span>
nc -l -p 2000 -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>nc [ip|hostname] 3000<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## TCP -&gt; UDP</span>
nc -l -p 2000 -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>nc -u [ip|hostname] 3000<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## UDP -&gt; UDP</span>
nc -l -u -p 2000 -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>nc -u [ip|hostname] 3000<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>## UDP -&gt; TCP</span>
nc -l -u -p 2000 -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>nc [ip|hostname] 3000<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-gnutls-cli" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-gnutls-cli"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://gnutls.org/manual/html_node/gnutls_002dcli-Invocation.html" rel="nofollow">gnutls-cli</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-connection-to-remote-host-with-sni-support" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-connection-to-remote-host-with-sni-support"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing connection to remote host (with SNI support)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>gnutls-cli -p 443 google.com</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-connection-to-remote-host-without-sni-support" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-connection-to-remote-host-without-sni-support"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing connection to remote host (without SNI support)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>gnutls-cli --disable-sni -p 443 google.com</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-socat" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-socat"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://www.dest-unreach.org/socat/doc/socat.html" rel="nofollow">socat</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-testing-remote-connection-to-port-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#testing-remote-connection-to-port-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Testing remote connection to port</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>socat - TCP4:10.240.30.3:22</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-</code> - standard input (STDIO)</li>
<li><code>TCP4:&lt;params&gt;</code> - set tcp4 connection with specific params
<ul>
<li><code>[hostname|ip]</code> - set hostname/ip</li>
<li><code>[1-65535]</code> - set port number</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-redirecting-tcp-traffic-to-a-unix-domain-socket-under-linux" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#redirecting-tcp-traffic-to-a-unix-domain-socket-under-linux"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Redirecting TCP-traffic to a UNIX domain socket under Linux</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>socat TCP-LISTEN:1234,bind=127.0.0.1,reuseaddr,fork,su=nobody,range=127.0.0.0/8 UNIX-CLIENT:/tmp/foo</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>TCP-LISTEN:&lt;params&gt;</code> - set tcp listen with specific params
<ul>
<li><code>[1-65535]</code> - set port number</li>
<li><code>bind=[hostname|ip]</code> - set bind hostname/ip</li>
<li><code>reuseaddr</code> - allows other sockets to bind to an address</li>
<li><code>fork</code> - keeps the parent process attempting to produce more connections</li>
<li><code>su=nobody</code> - set user</li>
<li><code>range=[ip-range]</code> - ip range</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li><code>UNIX-CLIENT:&lt;params&gt;</code> - communicates with the specified peer socket
<ul>
<li><code>filename</code> - define socket</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-p0f" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-p0f"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://lcamtuf.coredump.cx/p0f3/" rel="nofollow">p0f</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-set-iface-in-promiscuous-mode-and-dump-traffic-to-the-log-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#set-iface-in-promiscuous-mode-and-dump-traffic-to-the-log-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Set iface in promiscuous mode and dump traffic to the log file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>p0f -i enp0s25 -p -d -o /dump/enp0s25.log</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>-i</code> - listen on the specified interface</li>
<li><code>-p</code> - set interface in promiscuous mode</li>
<li><code>-d</code> - fork into background</li>
<li><code>-o</code> - output file</li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-netstat" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-netstat"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netstat" rel="nofollow">netstat</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-graph--of-connections-for-each-hosts" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#graph--of-connections-for-each-hosts"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Graph # of connections for each hosts</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>netstat -an <span class="pl-k">|</span> awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/ESTABLISHED/ { split($5,ip,":"); if (ip[1] !~ /^$/) print ip[1] }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sort <span class="pl-k">|</span> uniq -c <span class="pl-k">|</span> awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{ printf("%s\t%s\t",$2,$1) ; for (i = 0; i &lt; $1; i++) {printf("*")}; print "" }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-monitor-open-connections-for-specific-port-including-listen-count-and-sort-it-per-ip" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#monitor-open-connections-for-specific-port-including-listen-count-and-sort-it-per-ip"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Monitor open connections for specific port including listen, count and sort it per IP</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>watch <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>netstat -plan | grep :443 | awk {'print <span class="pl-cce">\$</span>5'} | cut -d: -f 1 | sort | uniq -c | sort -nk 1<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-grab-banners-from-local-ipv4-listening-ports" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#grab-banners-from-local-ipv4-listening-ports"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Grab banners from local IPv4 listening ports</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>netstat -nlt <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>tcp <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> grep -Eo <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>[1-9][0-9]*<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> xargs -I {} sh -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>echo <span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span> | nc -v -n -w1 127.0.0.1 {}<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
