<h5><a id="user-content-tool-rsync" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-rsync"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rsync" rel="nofollow">rsync</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-rsync-remote-data-as-root-using-sudo" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#rsync-remote-data-as-root-using-sudo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Rsync remote data as root using sudo</h6>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-host" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-host"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Host_(Unix)" rel="nofollow">host</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-resolves-the-domain-name-using-external-dns-server" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#resolves-the-domain-name-using-external-dns-server"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Resolves the domain name (using external dns server)</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-checks-the-domain-administrator-soa-record" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#checks-the-domain-administrator-soa-record"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Checks the domain administrator (SOA record)</h6>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-dig" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-dig"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dig_(command)" rel="nofollow">dig</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-resolves-the-domain-name-short-output" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#resolves-the-domain-name-short-output"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Resolves the domain name (short output)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>dig google.com +short</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-lookup-ns-record-for-specific-domain" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#lookup-ns-record-for-specific-domain"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Lookup NS record for specific domain</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>dig @9.9.9.9 google.com NS</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-query-only-answer-section" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#query-only-answer-section"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Query only answer section</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>dig google.com +nocomments +noquestion +noauthority +noadditional +nostats</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-query-all-dns-records" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#query-all-dns-records"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Query ALL DNS Records</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>dig google.com ANY +noall +answer</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-dns-reverse-look-up" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#dns-reverse-look-up"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>DNS Reverse Look-up</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>dig -x 172.217.16.14 +short</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-certbot" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-certbot"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://certbot.eff.org/" rel="nofollow">certbot</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-multidomain-certificate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-multidomain-certificate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate multidomain certificate</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>certbot certonly -d example.com -d www.example.com</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-wildcard-certificate" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-wildcard-certificate"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate wildcard certificate</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>certbot certonly --manual --preferred-challenges=dns -d example.com -d <span class="pl-k">*</span>.example.com</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-generate-certificate-with-4096-bit-private-key" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#generate-certificate-with-4096-bit-private-key"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Generate certificate with 4096 bit private key</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>certbot certonly -d example.com -d www.example.com --rsa-key-size 4096</pre></div>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-network-other" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-network-other"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://github.com/trimstray/the-book-of-secret-knowledge#tool-network-other">network-other</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-get-all-subnets-for-specific-as-autonomous-system" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#get-all-subnets-for-specific-as-autonomous-system"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Get all subnets for specific AS (Autonomous system)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>AS=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>AS32934<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
whois -h whois.radb.net -- <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>-i origin <span class="pl-smi">${AS}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>^route:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
cut -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -f2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sed -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/^[ \t]//<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sort -n -t <span class="pl-c1">.</span> -k 1,1 -k 2,2 -k 3,3 -k 4,4 <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
cut -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>:<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> -f2 <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sed -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/^[ \t]/allow /<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sed <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/$/;/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \
sed <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/allow  */subnet -&gt; /g<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-resolves-domain-name-from-dnsgooglecom-with-curl-and-jq" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#resolves-domain-name-from-dnsgooglecom-with-curl-and-jq"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Resolves domain name from dns.google.com with curl and jq</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>_dname=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>google.com<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> curl -s <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://dns.google.com/resolve?name=<span class="pl-smi">${_dname}</span>&amp;type=A<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> jq <span class="pl-c1">.</span></pre></div>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-git" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-git"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://git-scm.com/" rel="nofollow">git</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-log-alias-for-a-decent-view-of-your-repo" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#log-alias-for-a-decent-view-of-your-repo"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Log alias for a decent view of your repo</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 1)</span>
git log --oneline --decorate --graph --all

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> 2)</span>
git log --graph \
--pretty=format:<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>%Cred%h%Creset -%C(yellow)%d%Creset %s %Cgreen(%cr) %C(bold blue)&lt;%an&gt;%Creset<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
--abbrev-commit</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-python" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-python"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.python.org/" rel="nofollow">python</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-static-http-web-server-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#static-http-web-server-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Static HTTP web server</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Python 3.x</span>
python3 -m http.server 8000 --bind 127.0.0.1

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Python 2.x</span>
python -m SimpleHTTPServer 8000</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-static-http-web-server-with-ssl-support" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#static-http-web-server-with-ssl-support"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Static HTTP web server with SSL support</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Python 3.x</span>
from http.server import HTTPServer, BaseHTTPRequestHandler
import ssl

httpd = HTTPServer<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">((</span>'localhost'<span class="pl-k">,</span> <span class="pl-c1">4443</span>)<span class="pl-k">,</span> BaseHTTPRequestHandler)</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">httpd.socket = ssl.wrap_socket (httpd.socket,</span>
<span class="pl-s">        keyfile="path/to/key.pem",</span>
<span class="pl-s">        certfile='path/to/cert.pem', server_side=True)</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">httpd.serve_forever()</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s"># Python <span class="pl-c1">2</span>.x</span>
<span class="pl-s">import BaseHTTPServer, SimpleHTTPServer</span>
<span class="pl-s">import ssl</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">httpd = BaseHTTPServer.HTTPServer(('localhost', <span class="pl-c1">4443</span>),</span>
<span class="pl-s">        SimpleHTTPServer.SimpleHTTPRequestHandler)</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">httpd.socket = ssl.wrap_socket (httpd.socket,</span>
<span class="pl-s">        keyfile="path/tp/key.pem",</span>
<span class="pl-s">        certfile='path/to/cert.pem', server_side=True)</span>
<span class="pl-s"></span>
<span class="pl-s">httpd.serve_forever()</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-encode-base64" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#encode-base64"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Encode base64</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>python -m base64 -e <span class="pl-k">&lt;&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>sample string<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-decode-base64" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#decode-base64"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Decode base64</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>python -m base64 -d <span class="pl-k">&lt;&lt;&lt;</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>dGhpcyBpcyBlbmNvZGVkCg==<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span></pre></div>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-awk" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-awk"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://www.grymoire.com/Unix/Awk.html" rel="nofollow">awk</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-search-for-matching-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#search-for-matching-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Search for matching lines</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> egrep foo</span>
awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/foo/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-search-non-matching-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#search-non-matching-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Search non matching lines</h6>

awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>!/foo/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-matching-lines-with-numbers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-matching-lines-with-numbers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print matching lines with numbers</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> egrep -n foo</span>
awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/foo/{print FNR,$0}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-the-last-column" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-the-last-column"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print the last column</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{print $NF}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-find-all-the-lines-longer-than-80-characters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#find-all-the-lines-longer-than-80-characters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Find all the lines longer than 80 characters</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>length($0)&gt;80{print FNR,$0}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-only-lines-of-less-than-80-characters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-only-lines-of-less-than-80-characters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print only lines of less than 80 characters</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>length &lt; 80 filename</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-double-new-lines-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-double-new-lines-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print double new lines a file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>1; { print "" }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-line-numbers" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-line-numbers"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print line numbers</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{ print FNR "\t" $0 }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename
awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{ printf("%5d : %s\n", NR, $0) }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename   <span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> in a fancy manner</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-line-numbers-for-only-non-blank-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-line-numbers-for-only-non-blank-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print line numbers for only non-blank lines</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>NF { $0=++a " :" $0 }; { print }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-the-line-and-the-next-two-i5-lines-after-the-line-matching-regexp" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-the-line-and-the-next-two-i5-lines-after-the-line-matching-regexp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print the line and the next two (i=5) lines after the line matching regexp</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/foo/{i=5+1;}{if(i){i--; print;}}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-the-lines-starting-at-the-line-matching-server--until-the-line-matching-" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-the-lines-starting-at-the-line-matching-server--until-the-line-matching-"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print the lines starting at the line matching 'server {' until the line matching '}'</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/server {/,/}/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-multiple-columns-with-separators" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-multiple-columns-with-separators"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print multiple columns with separators</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk -F<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span> <span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{print "ip:\t" $2 "\n port:\t" $3<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-remove-empty-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-empty-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove empty lines</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>NF &gt; 0<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> alternative:</span>
awk NF filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-delete-trailing-white-space-spaces-tabs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#delete-trailing-white-space-spaces-tabs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Delete trailing white space (spaces, tabs)</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{sub(/[ \t]*$/, "");print}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-delete-leading-white-space" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#delete-leading-white-space"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Delete leading white space</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{sub(/^[ \t]+/, ""); print}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-remove-duplicate-consecutive-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-duplicate-consecutive-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove duplicate consecutive lines</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> uniq</span>
awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>a !~ $0{print}; {a=$0}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-remove-duplicate-entries-in-a-file-without-sorting" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-duplicate-entries-in-a-file-without-sorting"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove duplicate entries in a file without sorting</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>!x[$0]++<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-exclude-multiple-columns" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#exclude-multiple-columns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Exclude multiple columns</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>{$1=$3=""}1<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-substitute-foo-for-bar-on-lines-matching-regexp" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#substitute-foo-for-bar-on-lines-matching-regexp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Substitute foo for bar on lines matching regexp</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/regexp/{gsub(/foo/, "bar")};{print}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-add-some-characters-at-the-beginning-of-matching-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#add-some-characters-at-the-beginning-of-matching-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Add some characters at the beginning of matching lines</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/regexp/{sub(/^/, "++++"); print;next;}{print}<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-get-the-last-hour-of-apache-logs" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#get-the-last-hour-of-apache-logs"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Get the last hour of Apache logs</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>awk <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>1 hours ago<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>+%d<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>/%b<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>/%Y:%H:%M<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/,/<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>date <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>+%d<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>/%b<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>/%Y:%H:%M<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/ { print $0 }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> \
/var/log/httpd/access_log</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-sed" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-sed"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://www.grymoire.com/Unix/Sed.html" rel="nofollow">sed</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-print-a-specific-line-from-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#print-a-specific-line-from-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Print a specific line from a file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>sed -n 10p /path/to/file</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-remove-a-specific-line-from-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-a-specific-line-from-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove a specific line from a file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>sed -i 10d /path/to/file
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> alternative (BSD): sed -i'' 10d /path/to/file</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-remove-a-range-of-lines-from-a-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-a-range-of-lines-from-a-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove a range of lines from a file</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>sed -i <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span>file<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> -re <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>&lt;start&gt;,&lt;end&gt;d<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-replace-newlines-with-a-space" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#replace-newlines-with-a-space"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Replace newline(s) with a space</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>sed <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>:a;N;$!ba;s/\n/ /g<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> /path/to/file

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> cross-platform compatible syntax:</span>
sed -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>:a<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>N<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>$!ba<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/\n/ /g<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> /path/to/file</pre></div>
<ul>
<li><code>:a</code> create a label <code>a</code></li>
<li><code>N</code> append the next line to the pattern space</li>
<li><code>$!</code> if not the last line, ba branch (go to) label <code>a</code></li>
<li><code>s</code> substitute, <code>/\n/</code> regex for new line, <code>/ /</code> by a space, <code>/g</code> global match (as many times as it can)</li>
</ul>
<p>Alternatives:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> perl version (sed-like speed):</span>
perl -p -e <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>s/\n/ /<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> /path/to/file

<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> bash version (slow):</span>
<span class="pl-k">while</span> <span class="pl-c1">read</span> line <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">do</span> <span class="pl-c1">printf</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>%s<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$line</span> <span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">done</span> <span class="pl-k">&lt;</span> file</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-delete-string-n-next-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#delete-string-n-next-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Delete string +N next lines</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>sed <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>/start/,+4d<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> /path/to/file</pre></div>
<hr>
<h5><a id="user-content-tool-grep" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-grep"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="http://www.grymoire.com/Unix/Grep.html" rel="nofollow">grep</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-search-for-a-pattern-inside-all-files-in-the-current-directory" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#search-for-a-pattern-inside-all-files-in-the-current-directory"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Search for a "pattern" inside all files in the current directory</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>grep -rn <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pattern<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
grep -RnisI <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pattern<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">*</span>
fgrep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>pattern<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">*</span> -R</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-only-for-multiple-patterns" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-only-for-multiple-patterns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show only for multiple patterns</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>INFO*<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span><span class="pl-cce">\'</span><span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>WARN<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename
grep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>INFO\|WARN<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename
grep -e INFO -e WARN filename
grep -E <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>(INFO|WARN)<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename
egrep <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>INFO|WARN<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-except-multiple-patterns" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#except-multiple-patterns"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Except multiple patterns</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>grep -vE <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>(error|critical|warning)<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-data-from-file-without-comments" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-data-from-file-without-comments"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show data from file without comments</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>grep -v ^[[:space:]]<span class="pl-k">*</span><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> filename</span></pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-show-data-from-file-without-comments-and-new-lines" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-data-from-file-without-comments-and-new-lines"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show data from file without comments and new lines</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-show-strings-with-a-dashhyphen" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#show-strings-with-a-dashhyphen"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Show strings with a dash/hyphen</h6>

grep -- -- filename

<h6><a id="user-content-remove-blank-lines-from-a-file-and-save-output-to-new-file" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#remove-blank-lines-from-a-file-and-save-output-to-new-file"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Remove blank lines from a file and save output to new file</h6>

<h5><a id="user-content-tool-perl" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#tool-perl"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Tool: <a href="https://www.perl.org/" rel="nofollow">perl</a></h5>
<h6><a id="user-content-search-and-replace-in-place" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#search-and-replace-in-place"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Search and replace (in place)</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-edit-of-conf-files-changing-all-foo-to-bar-and-backup-original" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#edit-of-conf-files-changing-all-foo-to-bar-and-backup-original"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Edit of <code>*.conf</code> files changing all foo to bar (and backup original)</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-prints-the-first-20-lines-from-conf-files" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#prints-the-first-20-lines-from-conf-files"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Prints the first 20 lines from <code>*.conf</code> files</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-search-lines-10-to-20" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#search-lines-10-to-20"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Search lines 10 to 20</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-delete-first-10-lines-and-backup-original" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#delete-first-10-lines-and-backup-original"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Delete first 10 lines (and backup original)</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-delete-all-but-lines-between-foo-and-bar-and-backup-original" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#delete-all-but-lines-between-foo-and-bar-and-backup-original"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Delete all but lines between foo and bar (and backup original)</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-reduce-multiple-blank-lines-to-a-single-line" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#reduce-multiple-blank-lines-to-a-single-line"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Reduce multiple blank lines to a single line</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>perl -p -i -00pe0 filename</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-convert-tabs-to-spaces-1t--2sp" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#convert-tabs-to-spaces-1t--2sp"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Convert tabs to spaces (1t = 2sp)</h6>

<h6><a id="user-content-read-input-from-a-file-and-report-number-of-lines-and-characters" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#read-input-from-a-file-and-report-number-of-lines-and-characters"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Read input from a file and report number of lines and characters</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>perl -lne <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>$i++; $in += length($_); END { print "$i lines, $in characters"; }<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> filename</pre></div>
<h4><a id="user-content-shell-functions-toc" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#shell-functions-toc"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Shell functions Â <a href="#anger-table-of-contents"><sup>[TOC]</sup></a></h4>
<h5><a id="user-content-table-of-contents-1" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#table-of-contents-1"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Table of Contents</h5>
<ul>
<li><a href="#domain-resolve">Domain resolve</a></li>
<li><a href="#get-asn">Get ASN</a></li>
</ul>
<h6><a id="user-content-domain-resolve" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#domain-resolve"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Domain resolve</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Dependencies:</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>   - curl</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>   - jq</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">DomainResolve()</span> {

  <span class="pl-k">local</span> _host=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">local</span> _curl_base=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>curl --request GET<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-k">local</span> _timeout=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>15<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  _host_ip=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span><span class="pl-smi">$_curl_base</span> -ks -m <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_timeout</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>https://dns.google.com/resolve?name=<span class="pl-smi">${_host}</span>&amp;type=A<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \</span>
<span class="pl-s">  jq <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>.Answer[0].data<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> tr -d <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-cce">\"</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>/dev/null<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">if</span> [[ <span class="pl-k">-z</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_host_ip</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [[ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_host_ip</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>null<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]] <span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>

    <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> -en <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Unsuccessful domain name resolution.<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">else</span>

    <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> -en <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_host</span> &gt; <span class="pl-smi">$_host_ip</span><span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">fi</span>

}</pre></div>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>shell<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> DomainResolve nmap.org
nmap.org <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> 45.33.49.119

shell<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> DomainResolve nmap.org
Unsuccessful domain name resolution.</pre></div>
<h6><a id="user-content-get-asn" class="anchor" aria-hidden="true" href="#get-asn"><svg class="octicon octicon-link" viewBox="0 0 16 16" version="1.1" width="16" height="16" aria-hidden="true"><path fill-rule="evenodd" d="M4 9h1v1H4c-1.5 0-3-1.69-3-3.5S2.55 3 4 3h4c1.45 0 3 1.69 3 3.5 0 1.41-.91 2.72-2 3.25V8.59c.58-.45 1-1.27 1-2.09C10 5.22 8.98 4 8 4H4c-.98 0-2 1.22-2 2.5S3 9 4 9zm9-3h-1v1h1c1 0 2 1.22 2 2.5S13.98 12 13 12H9c-.98 0-2-1.22-2-2.5 0-.83.42-1.64 1-2.09V6.25c-1.09.53-2 1.84-2 3.25C6 11.31 7.55 13 9 13h4c1.45 0 3-1.69 3-3.5S14.5 6 13 6z"></path></svg></a>Get ASN</h6>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre><span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span> Dependencies:</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>   - curl</span>
<span class="pl-c"><span class="pl-c">#</span>   - python</span>

<span class="pl-k">function</span> <span class="pl-en">GetASN()</span> {

  <span class="pl-k">local</span> _ip=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$1</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">local</span> _curl_base=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>curl --request GET<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>
  <span class="pl-k">local</span> _timeout=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>15<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  _asn=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span><span class="pl-smi">$_curl_base</span> -ks -m <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_timeout</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>http://ip-api.com/json/<span class="pl-smi">${_ip}</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">|</span> \</span>
<span class="pl-s">  python -c <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">'</span>import sys, json; print json.load(sys.stdin)["as"]<span class="pl-pds">'</span></span> <span class="pl-k">2&gt;</span>/dev/null<span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>

  _state=<span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">$(</span>echo <span class="pl-smi">$?</span><span class="pl-pds">)</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">if</span> [[ <span class="pl-k">-z</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_ip</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [[ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_ip</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">==</span> <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>null<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> ]] <span class="pl-k">||</span> [[ <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_state</span><span class="pl-pds">"</span></span> <span class="pl-k">-ne</span> 0 ]]<span class="pl-k">;</span> <span class="pl-k">then</span>

    <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> -en <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span>Unsuccessful ASN gathering.<span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">else</span>

    <span class="pl-c1">echo</span> -en <span class="pl-s"><span class="pl-pds">"</span><span class="pl-smi">$_ip</span> &gt; <span class="pl-smi">$_asn</span><span class="pl-cce">\\</span>n<span class="pl-pds">"</span></span>

  <span class="pl-k">fi</span>

}</pre></div>
<p>Example:</p>
<div class="highlight highlight-source-shell"><pre>shell<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> GetASN 1.1.1.1
1.1.1.1 <span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> AS13335 Cloudflare, Inc.

shell<span class="pl-k">&gt;</span> GetASN 0.0.0.0
Unsuccessful ASN gathering.</pre></div>
